- Network Architecture and Optimization:
- Contribute to the architectural planning and evolution of the network, incorporating segment routing as a key technology.
- Identify opportunities for optimization and enhanced performance using segment routing techniques, such as traffic steering, BSIDs and fast reroute mechanisms.
- Perform network assessments and recommend improvements to maintain network health and operational efficiency.
- Represent the LEO Network Engineering team by documenting and delivering network requirements to hardware and software development teams specifically in the areas of customer facing MEF 3.0 interface and networking design support requirements on data processing equipment

- Protocols and Standards:
- Maintain a deep understanding of industry standards and protocols related to segment routing, such as IS-IS, BGP, and MPLS.
- Stay updated with emerging trends and advancements in segment routing technologies, applying them to enhance network capabilities.

- Collaborate with the LEO team to diagnose and address network behaviors and incidents in a timely manner, minimizing service disruptions.
- Vendor and Solution Evaluation:
- Evaluate new networking hardware, software, and solutions that align with segment routing strategies and network growth plans.
- Collaborate with vendors to understand product roadmaps and provide feedback for feature enhancements.
- Documentation and Knowledge Sharing:
- Create and maintain detailed technical documentation, including network diagrams, configuration guidelines, and troubleshooting procedures related to segment routing.
- Prepare and deliver materials including presentations, reference documentation and test strategies for LEO network equipment and applications deployment and operation
- Share knowledge and mentor junior team members, fostering a culture of continuous learning and skill development.
- With LEO Network Engineers develop and oversee plans including product idea investigations, proof of concept, Service validation and product demonstrations in Telesat LEO labs

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Myticas is seeking a High-Speed Analog EDA/CAD Engineer with to support SiGE and CMOS research &amp; development and chip design.<br>\
<br>\
Description:<br>\
Seeking an High-Speed Analog EDA/CAD Engineer to support and develop SiGe and CMOS design solutions for the high speed analog ASIC design team. The engineer will be hands-on with all phases of tool flow including foundry interface, PDK installation and support, tool evaluation and installation, layout, archive and tapeout. The engineer must be an expert in analog and mixed-signal circuit design flows and tools. Tasks will include significant tool and PDK customization and design team support. The self-motivated engineer must be able to anticipate problems and devise effective solutions.<br>\
Responsibilities:<br>\
• Install, customize and support external vendor PDK’s for both SiGe and CMOS processes<br>\
• Install, customize and support Custom IC and RF CAD environment for the design of high-speed (10–40 Gb/s), broad-band, mixed-signal, integrated circuits for fiber-based wireline applications.<br>\
• Lead and contribute to the development of design standards, IC development processes, CAD tools and design flows.<br>\
• Execute and support layout efforts including archive and tapeout processes<br>\
Minimum Expertise Requirements:<br>\
• Expert in high-speed analog and mixed-signal IC design concepts and must demonstrate superior critical thinking skills, problem solving capabilities and engineering judgment.<br>\
• Fluent with analog EDA front and back end tools<br>\
o Cadence Virtuoso, ADE<br>\
o Strong SKILL programming a must<br>\
o Mentor Calibre (end user support and rule deck writing)<br>\
• Detailed understanding of advanced high-speed analog &amp; mixed-signal layout concepts<br>\
• FlexLM license management<br>\
• Strong UNIX/Linux knowledge<br>\
• Not required but preferred<br>\
o Perforce<br>\
o Ocean scripting and advanced modelling and simulation knowledge<br>\
o Linux OS support<br>\
Minimum Experience Requirements:<br>\
• 5 years of experience working as a high-speed analog &amp; mixed signal IC CAD professional is required<br>\
• IC Technologies: High-speed IC technologies, including CMOS and bipolar.<br>\
• IC Design Software:<br>\
o Experience with configuring, documenting, and maintaining high speed analog IC design flows is a must.<br>\
o Experience with transistor-level IC design and verification software, e.g. Cadence Composer, Cadence Virtuoso, Cadence Spectre, Virtuoso AMS, Mentor Calibre, Skill language, is a must.<br>\
• General understanding of digital physical design flows, e.g. RTL coding, place and route, DRC/LVS verification.<br>\
• Work Environment: Comfortable working in a fast-paced environment. Must be strong individual contributor, and also able to work as member of a small team. Must be able to support EPDA users and solve problems efficiently, effectively and rapidly.<br>\
Education Requirements:<br>\
• BS 5+ years<br>\
• MS 4+ years<br>\
• PhD 3+ year</span></span><br>\

<!\[CDATA\[ <span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="background-color: white;"><span style="font-family: Calibri , sans-serif;"><span style=""><span style="color: black;">Our client is seeking an experienced <strong>Data Consultant</strong> with expertise in both <strong>Data Architecture</strong> and <strong>Data Engineering</strong>. The ideal candidate will assess the current data landscape, define the <em>As-Is</em> and <em>To-Be</em> state, and design practical solutions and roadmaps that enhance automation, integration, and reporting capabilities across the organization.</span></span></span></span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="background-color: white;"><span style="font-family: Calibri , sans-serif;"><span style=""><span style="color: black;">This is a <strong>hands-on, delivery-focused role</strong>—ideal for someone who can architect, engineer, and optimize modern data ecosystems end-to-end.</span></span></span></span></span><br>\

<span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="background-color: white;"><span style="font-family: Calibri , sans-serif;"><strong><span style=""><span style="color: black;">Key Responsibilities:</span></span></strong></span></span></span><br>\

• Design and implement scalable data frameworks and roadmaps supporting analytics and automation.<br>\
• Build and optimize data pipelines, ETL processes, and integrations using SQL, Informatica, and related tools.<br>\
• Drive automation and process optimization to improve data reliability and performance.<br>\
• Enable and enhance self-service analytics and visualization with Power BI and/or Tableau.<br>\
• Collaborate with stakeholders to align data initiatives with business goals.<br>\
• Improve data flow (“openflows”) and ensure transparency across systems.</span></span></span></span></span><br>\
<br>\

<!\[CDATA\[ <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">We are looking for a Performance &amp; Optimization Specialist for one of our clients to perform network performance, monitoring, and analysis by collecting and analyzing information, identifying the abnormalities from sources in the domain of the customer solution, diagnosing root causes of performance issues, and recommending improvement for optimization actions (i.e., QoS Optimization, parameter tuning, SW Upgrades, etc.) to meet contractual KPI targets. They find problems that were not identified during testing. In addition to diagnosing network performance issues, the Performance &amp; Optimization Specialist generates daily/weekly/monthly reports related to technology aspects of the customer solution. The specialist performs short-term capacity utilization and traffic pattern assessments to evaluate impact on current and future architecture and recommend optimal network strategy for future traffic/capacity needs, leveraging automation techniques to reduce analysis time and other optimization related activities that involve repetition.<br>\
Required Soft skills:<br>\
a) Strong communication skills<br>\
b) Self starter who will use own deep technical expertise to assess the network configuration and come up with feature/parameter trial plan independently.<br>\
c) Ability to interact/engage customer for technical discussions, review of technical reports/analysis/recommendations<br>\
d) NAM Time zone support<br>\
<br>\
Required Technical Skill Set:<br>\
1\. Strong understanding of 5G NSA, SA (FDD &amp; TDD) and LTE.<br>\
2\. Past hands-on experience with trials/optimization projects for 5G NSA/SA with demonstrated experience on 5G Features for Coverage optimization (e.g. SRS Beamforming), Throughput optimization, Load balancing, layering and Traffic Steering from low to high bands..<br>\
3\. Past hands-on experience with trials/optimization projects for LTE with demonstrated experience on 4G Features for Data/VoLTE Drop call improvement, Load balancing, Layering and Traffic Steering from low to high bands.<br>\
4\. Ability to analyze internal syslogs, eNB/gNB EMIL/DCAP logs, TTI traces for quick troubleshooting and issue resolution for lab or field activities.<br>\
5\. Expertise with UE and eNB/gNB signaling log analysis (UU, X2, S1 signaling)<br>\
6\. Exposure with UE logging tools such as QXDM, XCAL, or equivalent and should be proficient with those tools.<br>\
7\. Experience with Actix post processing of DT logs.<br>\
<br>\
Job Responsibilities<br>\
1\. Performs critical (sometimes escalated) design and performance activities in customer projects independently (complex problem solving in projects and multi-vendor environments).<br>\
2\. Develops / Reviews and makes recommendations on network-wide Design covering Performance, Spectrum &amp; Capacity supported by Recommendations (within and across the region).<br>\
3\. Organizes field measurements and laboratory tests. Performs network audits, especially in cases where fault or problems exist.<br>\
4\. Optimizes networks with all components based on traffic trends and customer forecasts.<br>\
5\. Supports experts in developing network configuration file and interface analysis<br>\
<br>\
Project Specific Roles<br>\
1\. I. LTE LMS assessment and LTE Features evaluation and executing trials for Load balancing, traffic steering campaigns for movement from low to high bands.<br>\
II. LTE and VoLTE Drop call rate improvement via troubleshooting configuration issues, analysis of counters and coming up with trial plan for KPI improvement based on feature trials and parameter tuning (not look for RF shaping skillset)<br>\
III. 5G LMS assessment and 5G Features evaluation and executing trials for 5G DL/UL Throughput improvement, Coverage improvement and traffic steering from low to high bands.<br>\
IV. Troubleshooting hot topics via OSS KPIs, TTI traces, EMIL traces etc</span></span><br> \]\]>

<p>You will design scalable data models and machine learning pipelines, apply ML techniques in cloud environments, and work closely with stakeholders to prioritize features and align product development with business needs. <!\[CDATA\[ <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong>Description</strong></span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">We are a cutting-edge technology company specializing in advanced emissions monitoring and analytics. By operating proprietary satellite and aircraft sensors, and combining these with third-party data, we power an analytics pipeline that delivers actionable environmental and business insights.</span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">This pipeline enables us to:</span></span>\
<ul>\
<li style="margin: 0.0cm;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong>Identify and classify potential emission sources</strong> with precision.</span></span>\

<li style="margin: 0.0cm;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong>Provide intelligence to customers</strong> that drives innovation, compliance, and positive environmental outcomes.</span></span>\
</ul>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Our structured, distributed datastore underpins this work, housing acquired data, intermediate artifacts, and pipeline outputs—an asset of significant value to analysts and aggregators worldwide.</span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong>The Opportunity</strong></span></span><br>\

<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">You will act as both architect and builder of our next-generation data platform, implementing scalable analytical solutions. This role is ideal for a technical leader who thrives on complex data challenges and understands how foundational data systems drive product innovation.</span></span><br>\

<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong>What You’ll Do</strong></span></span>\

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">The Manager will serve as a <strong>Linux Subject Matter Expert (SME)</strong>, responsible for monitoring, maintaining, troubleshooting, and supporting high-performance computing (HPC) nodes that are critical to our client’s day-to-day operations. The role focuses on ensuring a secure, optimized, and highly available HPC environment, while delivering deep technical expertise and guidance to users and internal teams.</span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Candidates must be able to work onsite at least <strong>4 days per week</strong>.</span></span>\
<div style="margin-bottom: 8.0pt;margin-left: 0.0cm;margin-right: 0.0cm;margin-top: 0.0cm;text-align: center;">\
<hr></div>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong>Key Responsibilities</strong></span></span>\
\
<ul>\
<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Act as the primary technical expert for <strong>Linux-based HPC clusters</strong> – ensuring performance, capacity, and availability targets are met.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Identify, diagnose, and resolve complex second-level issues for hardware, software, network, VPN, and Linux environments; escalate as needed with full documentation.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Manage daily operations of Linux-based HPC environments, including patching, upgrades, security hardening, and configuration of Ubuntu and RedHat systems.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Support job submission and workload management using <strong>Slurm</strong> or OpenHPC, and assist end users in optimizing compute workloads.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Migrate existing nodes to Linux, ensuring minimal downtime and performance impact.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Implement and manage cluster patching/automation tools such as <strong>Foreman</strong> (or similar) to streamline operations.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Install and configure servers, storage, hypervisors (KVM), and other HPC infrastructure components.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Automate administrative tasks to improve operational efficiency.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Execute firewall access requests, monitor security alerts, and assist in incident response.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Provide second-level support and mentorship to junior technical staff, ensuring knowledge transfer and consistent process execution.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Develop, maintain, and publish technical documentation, KB articles, and end-user guides for new systems or upgrades.</span></span>\

</ul>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">The HPC Administrator will serve as a <strong>Linux Subject Matter Expert (SME)</strong>, responsible for monitoring, maintaining, troubleshooting, and supporting high-performance computing (HPC) nodes that are critical to our client’s day-to-day operations. The role focuses on ensuring a secure, optimized, and highly available HPC environment, while delivering deep technical expertise and guidance to users and internal teams.</span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Candidates must be able to work onsite at least <strong>4 days per week</strong>.</span></span>\

<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Identify, diagnose, and resolve complex second-level issues for hardware, software, network, VPN, and Linux environments; escalate as needed with full documentation.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Manage daily operations of Linux-based HPC environments, including patching, upgrades, security hardening, and configuration of Ubuntu and RedHat systems.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Support job submission and workload management using <strong>Slurm</strong> or OpenHPC, and assist end users in optimizing compute workloads.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Migrate existing nodes to Linux, ensuring minimal downtime and performance impact.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Implement and manage cluster patching/automation tools such as <strong>Foreman</strong> (or similar) to streamline operations.</span></span>\

<li style="margin: 0.0cm 0.0cm 8.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Automate administrative tasks to improve operational efficiency.</span></span>\

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <p>We are seeking an experienced and highly skilled Senior Network Architect with expertise in Segment Routing to join our dynamic and innovative team. As a Senior Network Architect, you will play a pivotal role in designing, implementing, and optimizing our network infrastructure, with a specific focus on segment routing technologies. Your deep understanding of network architecture, protocols, and best practices will contribute to the scalability, reliability, and performance of our network while ensuring alignment with business objectives.</p>\
\
<p><br>\
The Sr. Network Architect is a Subject Matter Expert (SME) on all aspects of the LEO Network design and works with other LEO teams within Telesat and external contractors to ensure designs, implementation decisions, validation plans and documentation reflect the business requirements and objectives of the LEO program.</p>\
\
<h2>Main Responsibilities</h2>\
\
<ul>\
<li>Segment Routing Design and Implementation:</li>\
<li>Participate in the design and implementation of segment routing solutions, ensuring optimal utilization of network resources and improved traffic engineering.</li>\
<li>Collaborate with cross-functional teams to understand business requirements and translate them into effective network solution designs.</li>\
<li>Develop strategies for partner business units to implement and manage network services implementations of segment routing architectures.</li>\
<li>Network Architecture and Optimization:</li>\
<li>Contribute to the architectural planning and evolution of the network, incorporating segment routing as a key technology.</li>\
<li>Identify opportunities for optimization and enhanced performance using segment routing techniques, such as traffic steering, BSIDs and fast reroute mechanisms.</li>\
<li>Perform network assessments and recommend improvements to maintain network health and operational efficiency.</li>\
<li>Represent the LEO Network Engineering team by documenting and delivering network requirements to hardware and software development teams specifically in the areas of customer facing MEF 3.0 interface and networking design support requirements on data processing equipment</li>\
<li>In coordination with Network team attend, contribute and produce materials for internal and external design and system engineering reviews for LEO Network Engineering related activities</li>\
<li>Protocols and Standards:</li>\
<li>Maintain a deep understanding of industry standards and protocols related to segment routing, such as IS-IS, BGP, and MPLS.</li>\
<li>Stay updated with emerging trends and advancements in segment routing technologies, applying them to enhance network capabilities.</li>\
<li>Troubleshooting and Problem Resolution:</li>\
<li>Act as a subject matter expert, assist with complex network troubleshooting and incident resolution.</li>\
<li>Collaborate with the LEO team to diagnose and address network behaviors and incidents in a timely manner, minimizing service disruptions.</li>\
<li>Vendor and Solution Evaluation:</li>\
<li>Evaluate new networking hardware, software, and solutions that align with segment routing strategies and network growth plans.</li>\
<li>Collaborate with vendors to understand product roadmaps and provide feedback for feature enhancements.</li>\
<li>Documentation and Knowledge Sharing:</li>\
<li>Create and maintain detailed technical documentation, including network diagrams, configuration guidelines, and troubleshooting procedures related to segment routing.</li>\
<li>Prepare and deliver materials including presentations, reference documentation and test strategies for LEO network equipment and applications deployment and operation</li>\
<li>Share knowledge and mentor junior team members, fostering a culture of continuous learning and skill development.</li>\
<li>With LEO Network Engineers develop and oversee plans including product idea investigations, proof of concept, Service validation and product demonstrations in Telesat LEO labs</li>\
</ul>\
\
<h2>Education and Experience</h2>\
\
<ul>\
<li>10+ years of experience in carrier network design, operation and deployment</li>\
<li>Broad experience or exposure across all areas of network related product design, development, verification, deployment and support</li>\
<li>Understanding of Metro Ethernet Forum (MEF) standards and objectives as they relate to Carrier Ethernet Services.</li>\
<li>Knowledge of routing and switching protocols, including BGP, OSPF, IS-IS, and MPLS.</li>\
<li>Experience with network automation and scripting using tools such as Python, Ansible, or similar.</li>\
<li>Strong troubleshooting skills and the ability to diagnose and resolve complex network issues.</li>\
<li>Demonstrated leadership skills and the ability to guide and mentor junior engineers.</li>\
<li>In-depth understanding of security principles and practices as they relate to network architecture.</li>\
<li>Proven experience in network design, architecture, and optimization.</li>\
<li>Professional certifications such as Cisco CCIE, Juniper JNCIE, or equivalent, are highly desirable.</li>\
<li>Comfortable leading meetings and able to communicate issues and trends to senior management and other groups at the appropriate level of detail.</li>\
<li>Excellent communication (verbal, written, presentation) and interpersonal skills.</li>\
<li>Excellent communication and collaboration abilities, with a proven track record of working effectively within cross-functional teams.</li>\
<li>Communicates well with own team and across organizational boundaries to ensure the successful completion of shared goals.</li>\
</ul> \]\]>

...

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <p>We’re seeking an experienced <strong>SAP EWM Lead</strong> to drive warehousing design and delivery for a large S/4HANA program. This role is a long term, client-facing, hands-on, and requires frequent onsite presence in Winnipeg.</p>\

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <p>We are seeking a <strong>Network Verification &amp; Test Engineer</strong> to validate the performance, reliability, and compliance of advanced networking systems. This role involves creating verification plans, executing system-level tests, automating configurations, and working with industry-standard traffic generation tools. The ideal candidate will bring a strong networking background, hands-on testing expertise, and the ability to work both independently and in collaborative team settings.</p>\
\
<hr>\
<h3><strong>Key Responsibilities</strong></h3>\
\
<ul>\
<li>\
<p>Develop <strong>system and subsystem verification matrices</strong> to ensure full coverage of all system requirements.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Coordinate and participate in <strong>system-level testing activities</strong>, including planning, execution, and reporting of results.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Design, develop, and maintain <strong>test cases</strong> and <strong>test beds</strong> to support various testing scenarios.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Execute tests using traffic generators (e.g., Spirent, IXIA, Test Center), packet capture tools (tcpdump), and performance tools (iPerf).</p>\
<li>\
<p>Validate networking features and performance across <strong>OSI layers</strong>, including TCP, UDP, IP networking, routing protocols, and network optimization techniques.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Implement and manage <strong>NETCONF</strong> and <strong>gRPC/gNMI</strong> for automated network device configuration.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Work with structured <strong>data formats</strong> such as JSON, JSON IETF, XML, YAML, PROTO, and <strong>REST APIs</strong> to support automation workflows.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Utilize <strong>Kubernetes (POD)</strong> and <strong>Docker</strong> containers for test environment setup and management.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Troubleshoot and resolve performance and functional issues, ensuring timely defect identification and resolution.</p>\
</ul>\
\
<hr>\
<h3><strong>Required Qualifications</strong></h3>\
\
<ul>\
<li>\
<p>Proven experience with <strong>traffic generation and analysis tools</strong> such as Spirent, IXIA, Test Center, tcpdump, and iPerf.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Strong understanding of <strong>networking fundamentals</strong>, including OSI layers, TCP/UDP/IP protocols, routing protocols, and optimization methods.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Experience configuring and automating network devices using <strong>NETCONF</strong> and <strong>gRPC/gNMI</strong>.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Proficiency with structured data formats (JSON, XML, YAML, PROTO) and <strong>REST API</strong> integration.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Familiarity with <strong>Kubernetes</strong> and <strong>Docker</strong> environments.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Strong <strong>problem-solving</strong> and <strong>analytical</strong> skills.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Ability to work independently and within cross-functional teams.</p>\
</ul>\

<hr>\
<h3><strong>Preferred Qualifications</strong></h3>\
\

<li>\

<li>\
<p>Prior experience in <strong>network verification</strong>, <strong>system integration testing</strong>, or <strong>telecom/network equipment validation</strong>.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Exposure to performance benchmarking and large-scale test environments.</p>\
</ul> \]\]>

<p><strong><u>Job Summary:</u></strong><br>\
Serve as the lead <em><strong>OCM specialist for an enterprise-wide initiative in Information Security and Risk Management (ISRM) </strong></em>within BTS, focused on embedding secure coding practices from the outset of software and application development.<br>\

<li>Serve as a key advisor and change competency advocate, keeping leadership and stakeholders informed of risks, challenges, and achievements.\

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <p><strong>Myticas's direct client, based in Riverwoods, IL or Philadelphia, PA, is currently seeking a Accounting Manager</strong> <strong>for a hybrid contract to hire position.</strong></p>\
\
<p> </p>\
\
<p><strong>Additional Information</strong><strong>:</strong>  W2 only!</p>\
\
<ul>\
<li>Hybrid position - 2 to 3 days per week onsite, open to candidates local to Philadelphia, PA or Riverwoods, IL\
<li>This is a Temp-to-Hire Position\
</ul>\
\
<p><strong>Job Description:</strong></p>\
\
<p>The Accounting Manager plays a critical role in overseeing the accounting and financial reporting functions, ensuring accuracy, timeliness, and compliance with internal controls. This position requires a detail-oriented, analytical thinker with strong leadership capabilities and the ability to navigate complex accounting scenarios proactively.<br>\
<br>\
<strong>ESSENTIAL DUTIES AND RESPONSIBILITIES:</strong><br>\
• Lead and support the month-end close and reporting process in alignment with the reporting calendar.<br>\
• Supervise and mentor accounting staff, providing guidance, performance feedback, and support to improve processes — including the quality of account reconciliations.<br>\
• Review, analyze, and approve general ledger transactions to ensure completeness and accuracy.<br>\
• Oversee the preparation and review of balance sheet account reconciliations on a monthly, quarterly, and semi-annual basis.<br>\
• Proactively identify and resolve accounting issues, escalating, when necessary, with recommended solutions.<br>\
• Support internal and external audits by providing requested documentation and addressing inquiries professionally.<br>\
• Maintain and update desktop procedures and checklists to reflect changes in processes and tools.<br>\
• Maintain and monitor month-end close, reporting, and operational checklists to ensure timely and complete task execution before sign-off.<br>\
• Prepare and review supporting schedules and financial analyses as needed.<br>\
• Collaborate effectively with internal teams and third-party service providers to ensure smooth operations.<br>\
• Conduct independent analysis to identify opportunities for process improvement and implement recommendations.<br>\
• Support the timely research and resolution of reconciling items to ensure accuracy and compliance with deadlines.<br>\
• Demonstrate adaptability to changing business requirements and provide leadership and support to staff during transitions.<br>\
• Take initiative in identifying issues and opportunities, follow through on projects, and proactively recommend solutions to improve processes and resolve challenges.<br>\
<br>\
<strong>Required Qualifications/Experience/Skills: </strong><br>\
• 7–9 years of<strong> accounting/audit experience, including 2–3 years in a managerial</strong> role.<br>\
• Ideal candidates must have <strong>current or recent (within the past 1–2 years) experience managing teams responsible for core general ledger functions</strong>. This includes hands-on oversight of month-end close, journal entry preparation and review, balance sheet and bank reconciliations, intercompany transactions, and audit support.<br>\
• <strong>Bachelor’s degree in Accounting (BBA or BS)</strong>; Master’s degree preferred.<br>\
• <strong>CPA certification </strong>or progress toward certification strongly preferred.<br>\
<br>\
<strong>A strong and recent focus on GL is required to be considered for this role:</strong><br>\
• Experience with international accounting is a plus.<br>\
• Proficiency in major <strong>ERP systems (SAP, Great Plains, NetSuite) and Blackline.</strong><br>\
• Advanced skills in <strong>Microsoft Office Suite (Excel, Word, PowerPoint, Access).</strong><br>\
• Strong analytical and problem-solving skills with a detail-oriented approach.<br>\
• Proven ability to manage teams and work independently in a fast-paced environment.<br>\
• Comfortable working wit<strong>h accelerated month-end close timelines (3–5 days).</strong><br>\
• Excellent communication and interpersonal skills to foster cross-functional collaboration.<br>\
• Project management experience is highly desirable.<br>\
• Flexibility to work hybrid hours and coordinate effectively during close/reporting cycles.</p> \]\]>

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <p><strong>Title: </strong>Cyber Posture Management Analyst</p>\
\
<p><strong>Type: </strong>Direct Hire</p>\
\
<p><strong>Location: </strong>Lansing, Michigan</p>\
\
<p>Clover Consulting (a Myticas Co.) has a large, direct client seeking a skilled Cyber Posture Mgmt. Analyst I to join the team as part of their Information Security &amp; Privacy team. This position provides security analysis for the company's Identity and Access Management (IAM) Operation's program. This role requires knowledge across multiple platforms, applications, processes, and procedures to enable access management of business initiatives across the enterprise.</p>\
\
<p><strong><u>Essential Responsibilities</u></strong></p>\
\
<ul>\
<li>Familiar with identity and access management, with a focus on Privileged Access Management (PAM), Multi-Factor Authentication (MFA), and Identity Governance and Administration (IGA).\
<li>Knowledge of scripting languages (e.g., PowerShell, Python) for automation and customization of IAM solutions.\
<li>Understanding of identity protocols and technologies: OpenID Connect (OIDC,) OAuth, SAML, AD-Fed, API Gateways, SCIM, and platforms such as, Sailpoint, CyberArk, and MS Entra.\
<li>Knowledge of identity &amp; access management vulnerabilities, threats and mitigations.\
<li>Ability to determine how a security system works (including its resilience and dependability capabilities) and how changes in conditions, operations, or the environment will affect these outcomes.\
<li>Familiar with modern software life cycle development and automated cloud infrastructure deployment.\
<li>Understanding of network architecture, operating systems, and security protocols.\
<li>Ability to work independently and collaboratively in a fast-paced environment.\
<li>Supports initiatives and projects that will improve the organization’s cyber posture.\
<li>Excellent analytical and problem-solving skills.\
<li>Strong communication and interpersonal skills.\
<li>Understanding of security controls, risk management, and regulatory compliance (NIST CSF/SOX/GDPR/etc.).\
<li>Extended hours, including on-call may be required.\
</ul>\
\
<p><strong><u>Knowledge, Skills and Abilities</u></strong></p>\
\
<ul>\
<li>Ability to receive and incorporate feedback.\
<li>Strong verbal and written communication skills.\
<li>Strong attention to detail.\
<li>Strong interpersonal, analytical, and problem-solving skills.\
<li>Flexibility in day-to-day work.\
<li>Ability to learn the company’s supported systems and their interfaces with other systems.\
<li>Strong knowledge of Microsoft software applications.\
<li>Ability to communicate technical concepts in an understandable fashion.\
<li>Ability to prioritize multiple tasks and execute efficiently and effectively while demonstrating a clear sense of urgency when appropriate.\
<li>Excellent customer service focus and skills.\
<li>Ability to collaborate effectively in a team environment to achieve desired results.\
<li>Scripting knowledge preferred.\
</ul>\
\
<p><strong><u>Qualifications</u></strong></p>\
\
<ul>\
<li>Bachelor's Degree or equivalent experience and/or education required.\
<li>1+ years knowledge of financial products, regulatory requirements, and business process preferred.\
<li>Cloud Identity experience preferred.\
<li>SC-300 Microsoft Certified Identity and Access Administrator Associate preferred.\
<li>CISSP Certified Information Systems Security Professional preferred.\
</ul> \]\]>

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong>Materials Manager</strong><br>\
Location: Freer, TX<br>\
Pay Range: $45.00 - $50.00 per hour<br>\
Benefits: Standard Medical, Dental, 401(k)<br>\
Will be issued a fleet vehicle</span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><strong><u>Summary</u></strong><br>\
<br>\
The Materials Manager is responsible for managing the receiving, inspection, storage and transfer of all company and client procured materials and equipment to subcontractors at the various project sites. The Field Materials Manager may also direct the work of the Field Materials Coordinator, provide guidance, mentorship and facilitate their development.<br>\
<br>\
<strong><u>Responsibilities</u></strong></span></span>\
<ul>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Analyze and present the material status reports to validate and verify all shipments are delivered on schedule.  </span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Advise the Procurement team of any developments that may impact the project cost, schedule and client relationship.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Coordinate delivery schedules and timing between the job site and procurement.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Direct and oversee the receiving process for all incoming shipments of materials and equipment.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Implement, oversee and administer all project materials reporting processes and procedures including Material Receiving Reports (MRR) and Over, Short and Damaged reports (OS&amp;D) and distribute to the designated project and/or client personnel.</span></span>\
<li style="margin: 0.0in 0.0in 0.0in 0.5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;">Perform inspections of all materials delivered to the project site.</span></span>\

<!\[CDATA\[ <h1><strong>Senior Instrumentation &amp; Controls (I&amp;C) Design Engineer</strong></h1>\
\
<p>Location: <em>McCarran, NV<br>\
Direct hire <br>\
Compensation: 90,000-130,000</em></p>\
\
<hr>\
<h3> </h3>\
\
<hr>\
<h3><strong>Position Overview</strong></h3>\
\
<p>The <strong>Senior Instrumentation &amp; Controls (I&amp;C) Design Engineer</strong> will join the <strong>Infrastructure Development team</strong> to design and implement scalable, high-performance systems that support the company’s clean energy mission. This role is essential to advancing a <strong>circular economy for lithium-ion batteries</strong> by transforming recycled materials into high-quality inputs for new production.</p>\
\
<hr>\
<h3><strong>Key Responsibilities</strong></h3>\
\
<ul>\
<li>\
<p>Perform <strong>instrumentation and controls design assignments</strong> with minimal supervision.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Collaborate cross-functionally to develop <strong>technical solutions</strong> across all project phases.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Utilize <strong>Revit</strong> to produce detailed construction drawings, including:</p>\
\
<ul>\
<li>\
<p>Instrument and control panel layouts</p>\
<li>\
<p>Raceway drawings (conduit/cable tray sizing, routing, and fill calculations)</p>\
<li>\
<p>Circuit schedules for low-voltage control signals, power, and network wiring</p>\
<li>\
<p>Instrument wiring details, schedules, and installation details</p>\
</ul>\
<li>\
<p>Develop and maintain <strong>instrumentation installation specifications</strong>.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Coordinate with electrical engineers to size or adapt cable tray systems for I&amp;C applications.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Support controls engineering in the <strong>specification and selection</strong> of I&amp;C devices to ensure process and environmental compatibility.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Maintain accurate documentation, including <strong>datasheets, I/O lists, valve lists, and instrument lists</strong>.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Assist with <strong>procurement</strong> by reviewing vendor offerings and supporting component selection.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Contribute to process improvements, <strong>standard templates</strong>, and design workflows.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Support <strong>construction observation and administration</strong> to ensure quality and compliance.</p>\
</ul>\
\
<hr>\
<h3><strong>Qualifications</strong></h3>\
\
<ul>\
<li>\
<p><strong>Bachelor’s degree</strong> in Instrumentation &amp; Controls Engineering (or equivalent experience).</p>\
<li>\
<p><strong>4+ years</strong> of relevant I&amp;C design experience.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Highly motivated, proactive, and detail-oriented.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Strong organizational and communication skills.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Advanced proficiency in <strong>Revit, Navisworks, AutoCAD, Bluebeam</strong>, and <strong>Microsoft Office</strong>.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Working knowledge of <strong>UL508A</strong> standards for industrial control panel design and construction.</p>\
</ul>\
\

<!\[CDATA\[ <h1><strong>BESS Electrical Engineer</strong></h1>\
\
<p>Location: <em>San Francisco, CA</em><br>\
Direct Hire role <br>\
Compensation: Depending on experience but ranging from 130,000-190,000<br>\
</p>\
\
<hr>\
<h3><strong>About the Company</strong></h3>\
\
<p>A rapidly growing clean energy organization is building a localized battery supply chain that integrates recovery, reuse, and recycling of critical minerals. </p>\
\
<p>We are seeking a <strong>Battery Energy Storage Systems (BESS) Electrical Engineer</strong> to join our team. This role is central to designing scalable, high-performance energy storage infrastructure for both utility-scale and distributed applications. The mission is to build a sustainable circular economy for lithium-ion batteries by transforming recycled materials into high-quality inputs for new batteries.</p>\
\
<hr>\
<h3><strong>Key Responsibilities</strong></h3>\
\
<ul>\
<li>\
<p>Lead electrical engineering efforts for <strong>utility-scale lithium-ion BESS projects</strong>, from concept (system sizing, layout) through construction.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Interface with <strong>utilities and ISO/RTOs</strong> to support interconnection studies, permitting, and compliance.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Serve as internal <strong>subject matter expert (SME)</strong> for BESS-related technical challenges.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Design <strong>AC/DC electrical systems</strong> including transformers, inverters, combiners, and battery modules.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Develop schematic diagrams, single-line diagrams, wiring schematics, grounding, and protection strategies.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Specify and evaluate electrical components (breakers, contactors, fuses, EPO systems, meters).</p>\
<li>\
<p>Coordinate with <strong>civil, structural, SCADA, fire/life safety</strong>, and DC system teams for complete IFC packages.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Ensure compliance with <strong>NEC 705, NEC 706, IEEE 1547, UL 9540, NFPA 855</strong>, and local codes.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Support <strong>grid integration and interconnection</strong> with renewable and conventional sources.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Conduct <strong>power system studies</strong> (short circuit, load flow, arc flash, coordination).</p>\
<li>\
<p>Act as the <strong>Electrical Engineer of Record</strong> on assigned projects.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Stay current on <strong>BESS technologies, codes, and trends</strong>.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Lead <strong>R&amp;D initiatives</strong> on integrating BESS with MVDC distribution.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Provide <strong>construction administration support</strong> (RFIs, submittals, site inspections).</p>\
<li>\
<p>Track <strong>scope, schedule, and budget</strong> across stakeholders.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Prepare <strong>cost estimates and schedules</strong>; perform <strong>QA/QC</strong> reviews and mentor junior engineers.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Contribute to internal <strong>design standards, templates, and best practices</strong>.</p>\
</ul>\
\
<hr>\
<h3><strong>Desired Qualifications</strong></h3>\
\
<ul>\
<li>\
<p>Bachelor’s or Master’s degree in <strong>Electrical Engineering</strong> from an ABET-accredited program.</p>\
<li>\
<p><strong>Professional Engineer (PE)</strong> license in Nevada or eligible via reciprocity (must obtain NV and SC PE within 2 months).</p>\
<li>\
<p><strong>5+ years</strong> of experience in solar, energy storage, or microgrids; <strong>3+ years</strong> in BESS design/deployment.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Expertise in <strong>interconnection and regulatory compliance</strong> for BESS systems.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Advanced knowledge of <strong>NEC 705/706, IEEE 1547, UL 9540, NFPA 855</strong>.</p>\
<li>\
<p>Proficiency in:</p>\
\
<ul>\
<li>\
<p>Microgrid modeling (HOMER or similar)</p>\
<li>\
<p>Power system modeling (ETAP, SKM, or similar)</p>\
<li>\
<p>AutoCAD/Revit, Navisworks, Bluebeam, Microsoft Office</p>\
</ul>\
<li>\
<p>Preferred familiarity with:</p>\
\
<ul>\
<li>\
<p>PSSE/PSLF, PSCAD/EMTC</p>\
<li>\
<p>SEL AcSELerator or equivalent</p>\
<li>\
<p>HVDC and converter station design</p>\
</ul>\
<li>\
<p>Strong understanding of <strong>storage use cases</strong> (peak shaving, load shifting, demand/frequency response).</p>\
<li>\
<p><strong>Highly motivated, detail-oriented</strong>, and effective communicator.</p>\
</ul>\
\

<!\[CDATA\[ <span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Grid Systems Project Manager</span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Location: Charlotte, North Carolina (On-site/field)<br>\

<strong><u>Responsibilities:</u></strong></span></span>\

<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Apply industry experience and leading practices to architect, design, develop and implement SCADA, EMS, OMS, DMS, ADMS, and DERMS solutions to support complex business requirements.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Utilize in-depth knowledge of SCADA, EMS, OMS, DMS, ADMS, and DERMS to support commissioning, testing and deployment.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Provide field support, troubleshooting, and project coordination to enhance and maintain SCADA, EMS, OMS, DMS, ADMS, and DERMS.. This includes leading efforts in commissioning new SCADA systems and performing point testing and / or field data verification for advanced distribution applications such as FLISR, VVO, and DER Dispatch.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Lead or assist with program estimating, planning, and budgeting efforts and be accountable for the program/project delivery execution.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Support Analysis, Design, Build, Test, Triaging defects, Configuration, and Deployment activities. Ability to support Enterprise Program Management activities utilizing various methodologies such as but not limited to Waterfall and Agile methods.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Responsible for the successful completion of the project by budget, scope, quality, and attainment of the business objectives. In addition, supervise the overall project status and progress and ensure all scheduled milestones and delivery dates are met.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Responsible for overall project quality of deliverables.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Act as an application architect and solution architect, with responsibilities on the application and technical architecture teams.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Assist with or lead the business process design activities to drive out the complete application requirements: functional, quality, integration, and security.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Work with the application designer to create a high-level design of an end-to-end integration solution that provides a common structure for mapping the data between the applications.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Based on the activity and data flow diagrams, create an inventory of all cross-application interactions or interfaces, referred to as business events or messages.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Validate that the application requirements meet overall business process needs, are within the project scope, and are internally consistent.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Validate that the integration solution and integration architecture designs utilize the integration architecture components appropriately.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Lead or assist with completing high-level project communications and status reporting to the supporting executive team.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Assist with providing a central point of contact for all project interdependencies, internal and external.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Assist with the timely development and implementation of all stages of the system.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Use Project execution experience and knowledge to provide input and influence project execution processes and quality assurance/quality control protocols.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Ensure compliance with company and site safety policies.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">All other duties as assigned.</span></span>\
</ul>\
<span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;"><strong><u>Requirements</u></strong>:</span></span>\
\
<ul>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;"><strong>Bachelor’s degree in engineering, Business, Computer Science, Information Technology, or a closely related field from an accredited program and 8 years of relevant experience is Required.</strong> </span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Minimum 8 years of experience providing enterprise or operations architecture strategies, enterprise or operations integration solutions, and services leveraging various applications and technical platforms.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Minimum 5 years of GE e-terra ADMS experience, and 3 years of GE e-terra OMS.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Excellent enterprise architecture and integration skills, including data architecture, cloud architecture, middleware, communications, and other architectural methods and practices.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Experience in large-scale enterprise transformation projects using industry enterprise architecture strategy solutions and standard industry technologies.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Experience with electric utility clients implementing and integrating operational systems such as OMS, DMS, ADMS, AMI, Distribution Automation, and Distributed Energy Resources (DER) is preferred.</span></span>\

<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 11.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Experience with a variety of project execution methodologies including but not limited to Waterfall and Agile.</span></span>\

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <span style="font-size: 14.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;"><strong>Senior Automation &amp; Controls Engineer - Food &amp; Beverage</strong></span></span><br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Location: Atlanta, GA (On-site/field)<br>\
<br>\
Benefits: Access to Client Benefits Package<br>\
<br>\
<strong><u>Description:</u></strong><br>\
The Senior Automation &amp; Controls Engineer leads and executes Automation and Controls Engineering design activities for minor to major scale Engineering, Procurement, and Construction (EPC) projects in food, consumer products, pharmaceutical, life science, aerospace and industrial facilities.<br>\
<br>\
<strong><u>Responsibilities: </u></strong></span></span>\
<ul>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Responsible for compliance with company and project site safety policies. </span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Design responsibility for all Automation and Controls scope on the project.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Leads a team of Automation and Controls Engineers, Specialists, and Designers in the execution of design.  Interfaces with a multi-faceted project team internally consisting of project manager, electrical, controls, estimating, procurement, construction, and other engineering disciplines. </span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Responsible for leading and developing software design deliverables including PLC and HMI programming design deliverables as well as Batch, MES, servers and virtualization.  Responsible for commissioning and startup of those design deliverables. </span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Lead and prepare controls design deliverables, including instrument/device list, I/O list, controls narratives, control panel and controls hardware design, device location plan drawings and installation details.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Lead the specification, design, and procurement activities for control panel and equipment vendors, manage vendor progression, and lead the Factory Acceptance Tests (FATs).</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Lead and prepare electrical design deliverables including 480VAC and below equipment and motor power design, installation plan drawings, and conductor schedules.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Determine process instrument measurements protocols, such as temperature, pressure, flow, level, analyzers, and control valves. Utilize knowledge of various technologies for selecting the appropriate controls application.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Experienced in reviewing P&amp;IDs and working with process engineers to define and show proper controls scope of the project. </span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Develop and manage verification of design, calculations, project studies and report preparation.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Interfaces directly with offsite design office and coordinates and tracks execution of controls deliverables to that office.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Responsible for leading and performing quality reviews of project design submittals and coordinating those reviews within the department.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Responsible for applying knowledge of commonly used automation and controls engineering/design concepts, principles, practices, codes, and procedures within the engineering services industry. </span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Interfaces directly with construction personnel in development of contracts and execution of work.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Develops project estimates at each project phase through various software such as Proposal works, Integrated Architecture Builder (IAB), SIL Solver, Bluebeam, Excel, and Visio. </span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Supports project manager in the development and tracking of automation and controls project budgets and expected progress.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Works with clients and vendors directly in developing design. </span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Build effective relationships with existing clients, customers and contractors and develop new business opportunities. Responsible for ensuring customer satisfaction goals and expectations are met.  </span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Provides leadership, technical direction and development to Automation and Controls team members. </span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Assists in the day-to-day allocation of resources to their projects.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Coordinate with field personnel to resolve design related installation issues, calculations, field inspections and testing of controls systems. </span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Responsible for leading the technical execution and team during onsite start-up and commissioning activities.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Responsible for developing and submitting discipline change notices as needed to the project management team.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Fully understands and can execute the EPC project approach. </span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">This position will require making trips to job sites to survey, support installations, and lead startups <strong>(travel about 30%).</strong></span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Work with our business development team to identify and develop key projects and customer pursuits.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Frequently attends and hosts client events. </span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Develop business strategies for future projects.  Understands business needs and profitability factors. </span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Reviews and develop engineering hour estimates and proposals for all phases of the project. </span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Supports interviewing and hiring process for new team members.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Coordinates workload with Automation and Controls Department Manager.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Complies with all company policies and standards.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">All other duties as assigned.?</span></span>\
</ul>\
<br>\
<span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;"><strong><u>Requirements:</u></strong></span></span>\
\
<ul>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;"><strong>Bachelor’s degree</strong> in Controls, Electrical, Mechanical or Chemical Engineering or related degree from an ABET accredited program and <strong>successful completion of Fundamentals of Engineering (FE) exam</strong> and <strong>7 years electrical engineering experience</strong>. EPC project and Automation 7 Controls experience preferred.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;"><strong>Master’s degree </strong>in electrical engineering and <strong>6 years electrical engineering experience</strong>. EPC project experience preferred. </span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Expert knowledge in standard engineering techniques and procedures. Strong knowledge of electrical equipment design ANSI and IEEE Standards. Strong computer skills (e.g. Microsoft Office Suite).</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Excellent written and verbal communication skills.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Experience with leading the discipline design for large projects and delegating work tasks to team members. Ability to lead execution of work and resolve issues in a team environment.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Demonstrated critical thinking skills, ability to work methodically and analytically in a quantitative problem-solving environment.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Strong attention to detail, facilitation, team building, collaboration, organization and problem-solving skills.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Ability to perform quality reviews for detailed engineering documents and specifications.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Ability to travel. accredited program.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Must have or be able to obtain a Transportation Worker Identification Card (TWIC)</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Professional Engineer (PE) License Preferred</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Ability to perform quality reviews for detailed engineering documents and specifications.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Knowledge of applicable design standards covering Automation &amp; Controls Design/Engineering such as NFPA, ISA, IEC, IEEE, ISA/IEC 61511, ISO13849, UL508A.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Experienced with variety of control and safety systems (PLC, SCADA, SIS, BMS, DCS)</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Experience in Rockwell and Siemens PLC platform.  Experience in GE, Modicon, Opto22, Mitsubishi, and Triconex PLC platforms a plus.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">SCADA experience with Factory Talk and Wonderware local and distributed systems, Ignition Software is a plus.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">MES Design and Implementation Experience a Plus, PTC ThingWorx, Ignition/Sepasoft, Parsec TrakSYS.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Machine safety risk assessment and required PL design compliance to ISO13849 is a plus.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Process safety SIF/SIS design compliance to ISA/IEC 61511 is a plus.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Experience with PlantPAX and PackML is preferred.</span></span>\
<li class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0.0in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial , Helvetica , sans-serif;">Familiarity with tools like SISTEMA, CCW, IAB, BatchSIM, and PlantSIM is desired.</span></span>\
</ul>\

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <p><strong>Site Management Supervisor</strong><br>\
Location: Denver, CO / Hybrid</p>\
\
<p>Rate: $57.69-$72.11/hr.<br>\
Benefits: Medical, Dental, &amp; Vision</p>\
\
<p>\*\*\*\* This position includes a company vehicle with paid fuel. Candidate must be located within an hour of the Winter Park, CO area.</p>\
\
<p><strong>Qualifications:</strong></p>\
\
<ul>\
<li>Candidate must have a Level “A” wastewater license for the state of Colorado.\
<li>High school diploma.\
<li>6 years’ experience at an industrial water/wastewater treatment facility, or municipal water/wastewater facility public works operation, including experience in project management with responsibility for technical support and financial accountability or 6 years working in a related field.\
<li>Understanding of industrial operations including basic fluid flow, process equipment, and control instrumentation.\
<li>Three years of experience at a supervisory level.\
<li>Ability to travel 10% of the time.\
<li>Possess a valid driver’s license with no major infractions.\
<li>Proficient with computer software including Microsoft Suite (Word, Excel, Power Point, Outlook, Teams), PDF software, etc.\
<li>Ability to perform daily computer skills managing various client software programs, SCADA, and data entry.\
<li>Possess sufficient virtual communication skills to successfully maintain operations and regulatory compliance while located remote from client sites.\
<li>Candidate needs to be able to read, understand, and abide by Industrial Regulations and Standards.\
<li>Candidate needs to be able to read, understand, abide by, and guide their team in compliance with client safety, quality, and other requirements.\
<li>Candidate must live in Winter Park, CO, or a nearby community\
</ul>\
\
<p><strong>Responsibilities:</strong></p>\
\
<ul>\
<li>Manage staff for two locations in Colorado for a private-sector industrial client.\
<li>Organize and direct all onsite contract operations teams (projects) within the assigned portfolio.\
<li>Provide clients with effective performance in compliance with local, state, and federal regulatory agency water quality permit requirements.\
<li>Create a safe work culture and ensure safe work practices are followed by all staff.\
<li>Maintain assigned sites in Operational and Regulatory compliance.\
<li>Provide support, mentoring, training, and leadership to assure the highest possible effort on the part of onsite managers, local staff, and operators in the region.\
<li>Ensure staff stays on task and completes job related duties.\
<li>Assure personnel compliance with corporate reporting systems and customer reporting systems.\
<li>Lead O&amp;M personnel development and training program to drive professional advancement within the organization.\
<li>Implement O&amp;M training programs to develop all levels of associates at regional sites, recommend new training requirements, undertake to advance professional skills, mentor new project managers and members of the contract operating teams with a written plan.\
<li>Assure the implementation of all required training programs and performance reviews for new and existing projects.\
<li>Lead O&amp;M Safety, Maintenance, Process Control, cost/savings, process optimization, and Sustainability efforts in the assigned portfolio.\
<li>Participate in the selection, assignment, and orientation of all onsite supervisors and motivate extraordinary, self-starting effort by onsite supervisors.\
<li>Support affirmative action and diversity efforts in the assigned portfolio.\
<li>Assure O&amp;M management of the proper execution of job performance interviews and in the continuing communication of management policies to all personnel.\
<li>Develop all of the technical skills to function as an onsite manager and are prepared to perform these functions during project start up as well as during emergency situations.\
<li>Verify and complete all job-related documents and reports.\
<li>Maintain quality of operations and deliverables at the levels expected by client, including achievement of Key Performance Indicators (KPI) where applicable.\
<li>Frequently travel to sites for Client meetings, Inspections, and Operational Compliance.\
<li>Provide support with business development of contract operations and other efforts.\
<li>Report on all competitive contract services sales efforts and advises marketing personnel of these efforts and prepare other reports and presentations as required.\
<li>Provide primary client relationship with client management and technical personnel and report regularly as to client confidence, satisfaction, and/or problems.\
<li>Review monthly contract service reports for each installation, advising management as to project status, regulatory agency permit compliance, and technical/plant management attitudes.\
<li>Support regional personnel with the handling of local problems and in the development of client relations strategies to assure successful on-going business at each site.\
<li>Develop budgets and assist in the preparation of operations strategies to achieve compliance with regulatory agency requirements and O&amp;M corporate objectives.\
<li>Review all monthly project reports and utilize these materials to more effectively manage O&amp;M client services and to assure O&amp;M's compliance with all contract provisions and client understanding and satisfaction of services rendered.\
<li>Actively participate in regional and local professional groups, and reports on any technology or service advancements desired by local groups and/or O&amp;M clients.\
</ul>\
\
<p><em>We are an Equal Opportunity Employer and do not discriminate on the basis of race, color, religion, sex, national origin, age, disability, veteran status, genetic information, sexual orientation, gender identity, or any other legally protected status. All qualified applicants will receive consideration for employment without regard to any of these characteristics.</em></p> \]\]>
